<date>1606807836221< /date><rate>5< /rate><Review>This is the only bakery we will drive 25 minutes for their bread.  They have a large variety of pan dulce. The bread is continually coming out fresh. We come over at about 4 or 5pm and the turnovers are still warm! Super fresh!!

Do they have turnovers?!?!? A larger variety than most bakeries, including apple, pumpkin, caramel Dulce de Leche, guava, cream cheese, vanilla custard, strawberry, pineapple, and others. The best part is it always fresh and great tasting.

They also serve a variety of tortas, tamales and other Mexican food.  Tamales are large, delicious, and have lots of meat.  The pork loin and steak tortas are delicious with a strawberry milkshake, our usual order.

We have friends in Bakersfield requesting we bring pan dulce, caramel turnovers for grandma, and tricolor cookies for the kids every time we visit Bakersfield.</Review>< Pictures>

Their medium sized bowl generally leaves me full and happy for ten-spot, there is a large bowl for a few dollars more and a small for a couple less.

I went to Zin Nail with my nails in a very bad condition and they made them look all nice again.
